  //<![CDATA[
    function checkCB(chBox) {
      count = 0;
      first = null;
      f = chBox.form;
      for (i = 0 ; i < f.elements.length ; i++)
        if (f.elements[i].type == 'checkbox' && f.elements[i].checked) {
          if (first == null && f.elements[i] != chBox)
            first = f.elements[i];
          count += 1;
        }
      if (count > 2) {
        first.checked = false;
        count -= 1;
      }
    }
  //]]>
  </script>
